He is untrusting of Artanis and his warriors, upon first meeting them and has trouble letting go of the past. He is direct, and does not shy away from confrontation. He is an old warrior, whose deeds are remembered by the protoss to this day..

Loyal, proud, a champion of the protoss ideal, Fenix is the ultimate soldier of the protoss empire. The AI initially does not accept the fact that he is a replication of the personality he believes he is and throughout the story must come to accept this truth, carving out his own identity.

Character/Description/SelendisVoid=(Already Cast) Once a student of Artanis, Selendis has risen to the rank of Executor, the overall leader of the combined protoss military force. Her only superior is the Hierarch, her old teacher, only, Artanis. She is eager for the protoss to reclaim their homeland and represents the best and brightest of what the protoss can be--fiercely loyal to her race's ideals, completely dedicated and focused. However, over the years on Shakuras, Selendis has come to believe that the divided protoss tribes can never live in harmony and believes in returning her people to their former segregation.

Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00019=Es lo mejor que puedo hacer en el tiempo asignado. Tendrá que ser suficiente. /// It is the best I could do in the time allotted. It will have to be enough.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00020=Rezo para que el terrazine que extrajimos en Slayn sea suficiente para probar los límites de la piedra. /// I pray the terrazine we extracted while orbiting Slayn will prove sufficient to test the Keystone's limits.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00021=No te preocupes, Jerarca: la piedra está vacía. No aconsejo comenzar nuevas pruebas con formas de vida presentes. /// Do not worry, Hierarch, the Keystone is empty. It would be unwise to begin new tests with lifeforms present.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00022=Las energías del vacío son muy impredecibles. La piedra parece actuar como un punto focal, transformando la energía de una realidad en otra.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00023=No estoy seguro de que podamos progresar mucho más sin una fuente de energía del vacío, Jerarca. /// I'm not certain much more progress can be made without a significant source of Void energy, Hierarch.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00024=Mi investigación da cada vez menos frutos. Lo siento, Jerarca... pero me cuesta avanzar. /// My research grows more fruitless by the hour. I am sorry, Hierarch... But progress is slow.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00025=Intentar descifrar la piedra es casi una tarea de locos. Sin encontrar al menos un denominador común, se podrían generar resultados únicos y a la par válidos eternamente. /// Trying to decipher the Keystone is almost maddening. Without finding at least a single piece of common ground, one could create unique and yet valid results forever.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00026=La piedra resuena con las energías del vacío. Deberíamos investigar este fenómeno, Jerarca. /// The Keystone is resonating to Void energies below. We should investigate this further, Hierarch.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00027=¿Cuál podría ser la fuente de energía del vacío que emana de Slayn? ¿Los híbridos? Tiemblo de pensar en qué habrá abajo. /// What possible source of Void energy is emanating from Slayn? Hybrid? I shudder to think what lurks below.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00028=El terrazine ha pasado de gas a energía sin pérdidas ni añadidos... Increíble. /// The terrazine converted from gas to energy with no loss or gain... Incredible.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00029=Si la piedra se construyó para almacenar su punto de origen, debería estar expresado en un lenguaje que cualquier cultura pudiese interpretar. /// If the Keystone was constructed to store its origin point within, it would need to be expressed in a unifying language any culture could interpret.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00030=Su resistencia al deterioro es inconcebible. Ningún material se comportaría así... a menos que... /// This decay rate is impossible. No constructed material would behave this way... unless...
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00031=Claro... la forma física es un engaño. Eso significa que podría realinearse. /// Ah, yes. I see... the physical shape is a deception. That would mean it can be realigned.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00032=Al exponerla a las energías del vacío, la piedra comienza a absorberlas de inmediato, incluso desde gran distancia... Podemos aprovecharlo. /// When exposed to Void energies, the Keystone begins absorbing them immediately, even from a considerable distance... We can use this.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00033=Tiene que haber una forma de probar los límites de la capacidad de absorción de la piedra... ¿De dónde se obtiene energía del vacío? /// There must be a way to test the limits of the Keystone's absorption capabilities... Where does one acquire Void energy?
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00034=Interesante. Creo que la piedra es antiquísima. Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00035=Incluso estos resultados requieren más pruebas. /// Even these results require further testing.
Conversation/Response_Keystone/Line00036=Ahora mismo la piedra es bastante peligrosa, Jerarca. No deberías acercarte demasiado. /// The Keystone is quite dangerous at this moment, Hierarch. I would keep your distance for now.
